Suggestions:

2. The emergency handling skills of service personnel should also be trained. First of all, we must understand the pain points of guest complaints, right? Don't just think about shirking responsibility and keeping things quiet. An apology is necessary. Secondly, you can ask the guest if they need to clean again. If not, are there other remedial measures? Can you urgently change the room at the same price? Then deal with the evidence. This should be the initiative of the hotel, not the guest.
